  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6706f910-1a97-4496-a7a3-ed9575cfd3d5'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText597640677126302871" style="display:none"><b>Alice Brown</b> fell in love with Jack the day she moved into her freshman dorm. Problem is, she’s been stuck in the friend zone ever since. After another meaningless breakup, she’s ready to confess her feelings to Jack.<br /><br /><b>Jack Sullivan</b> has mistaken friendship for love once before and has vowed never to do it again. A varsity sports player, he’s determined to enjoy college with no strings attached.<br /><br /><b>Peter Wells</b> is Jack’s best wingman. He enjoys his popularity as team captain and when he meets Alice, he’s ready to steal her heart.<br /><br />When Jack sees Alice and Peter together, jealousy hits him hard. But will he break his vow to never date a friend?<br /><br /><b>Meet new characters and catch up with old ones in the second book in the <i>Just Friends</i> series.</b><br /><br /><i>Friend Zone</i> is part of the <i>Just Friends</i> new adult college romance series. Reading order:<br />Book 1 - <i>Let’s Be Just Friends</i><br />Book 2 - <i>Friend Zone</i><br />Book 3 - <i>My Best Friend's Boyfriend</i><br />Book 4 - <i>I Don't Want To Be Friends</i></span>

<div id="review_1904918622" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1904918622" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14045562-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542231656p2/14045562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1904918622?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/14045562-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14045562-amy?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1904918622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5765347206637745542">All of my reviews can be found on <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.novelgossip.com'>www.novelgossip.com</a><br/><br/>Actual rating 3.5/5<br/><br/>I loved the first Camilla Isley book I read, Love Connection so when I saw she was releasing a new book that was slightly different I was intrigued. LC focused on adult relationships whereas Friend Zone was about a group of college aged young men and women trying to navigate dating as well as friendships and school. I don’t read a ton of NA books but I have to say that I really liked this one! <br/><br/>There are several narrators her</span>
  <span id="freeText5765347206637745542" style="display:none">All of my reviews can be found on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.novelgossip.com">www.novelgossip.com</a><br /><br />Actual rating 3.5/5<br /><br />I loved the first Camilla Isley book I read, Love Connection so when I saw she was releasing a new book that was slightly different I was intrigued. LC focused on adult relationships whereas Friend Zone was about a group of college aged young men and women trying to navigate dating as well as friendships and school. I don’t read a ton of NA books but I have to say that I really liked this one! <br /><br />There are several narrators here, but the chapters are clearly labeled and it didn’t take me long to work out who was dating who and who lived with who. The two main protagonists are Alice and Jack. Alice has been in love with Jack since they met, but Jack is a player and he pushed Alice firmly into the friend zone straightaway. When Alice decides to try and forget about her feelings for Jack she starts dating his close friend and teammate, Peter. Of course Jack being a typical, clueless guy gets jealous and starts wondering if he should’ve dated Alice when had a chance. <br /><br />All of the characters here are attending Harvard and there’s a good mix of personalities and backgrounds. You have Alice and Jack who are both majoring in chemistry, Madison and Haley are Alice’s roommates and do computer coding and literature, respectively. Jack’s friends are mainly athletes, then there are a few chapters from Alice’s ex boyfriend Ethan and his new girlfriend Rose. It sounds like too much, but I promise it wasn’t confusing especially as they all interact with each frequently making it easy to establish their connections. I think that’s actually what set this apart from a typical story where friends turn to lovers for me. There were many side stories and relationships to follow and it kept me engaged. <br /><br />This was a really lighthearted and fun read, I’m all for some drama and they way they were hooking up and breaking up constantly made for some juicy scenes. Alice and Jack exchanged cute and playful banter that made me go awww, out loud a few times and I couldn’t help but root for them to figure it out and date each other already! Overall it was a cute and entertaining book that I read in a few hours. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5765347206637745542" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10387682389830908288"><b>Friend Zone (Just Friends #1)</b><br/><b>Background</b><br/>I like rom-com. I like love stories. I like them clean. But every 'romantic book series' that I have started in past three months, and there are <i>million</i>, mind you. They all have the same basic problem.   <span id="freeText10387682389830908288" style="display:none"><b>Friend Zone (Just Friends #1)</b><br /><b>Background</b><br />I like rom-com. I like love stories. I like them clean. But every 'romantic book series' that I have started in past three months, and there are <i>million</i>, mind you. They all have the same basic problem. Romance means getting naked as soon as opportunity strikes.<br /><br />Anyway, this time, for reasons I can't explain; I got two books of the series on same day. And this is a combined review for both - sort of.<br /><b>Review</b><br />Plot is about a few characters.<br />Rose and Tyler are childhood friends. Tyler has a girlfriend Georigina (Gigi). Gigi's brother is Ethan. Ethan is going out with Gigi's friend Alice. Alice's roommate is Madison... I am dozing off... but wait, let me finish this review.<br /><br />The first book was Rose and her relationship with Tyler and Ethan. <br />The story continues with Alice this time as she has the same twin relationship with Jake and Peter. But the story remains the same. <br /><br />A half 🌟 only for how she brought the two tracks book 1 and book 2 together. Cuz initially it feels like both stories are in parallel universes.<br /><br />Enough said.<br /><b>Verdict</b><br />2.5 stars. Don't bother if your likes and dislikes are like me.</span>

  <span id="freeText1376879776325405014" style="display:none">A friends to lovers love triangle with no cheating. This book was everything! The characters and emotions felt so real... I loved following the story from both Jack and Alice's POV.<br>Alice has had feelings for Jack since freshman year, but she's been stuck in the friend zone ever since. And if you've ever been "in the zone" you know how hard it is to watch your friend date... and how easy you wish each and every one of his reationships won't last... This is Alice for the past two years! But now she's just been dumped and Tyler had just dumped his latest fling so she's determined to not let another day go by without confessing her feelings to Jack. The only problem is she doesn't realize how scarred Jack is from another friendship-turned-relationship gone wrong... and so a series of epic misunderstandings begins... And they all felt very real... My eyes were glued to the pages I <i>had</i> to know what would happen next! The story kept evolving with so many twists and plot turns I hadn't seen coming, but the ending was SO satisfying... Also halfway through the new leading love story for the next book in the series is introduced and I must say I can't wait to read it. <br><br>I have to say that I didn't notice until the end that this was a second book in a series... but that didn't reduce my reading experience. Now the only problem I have is id to go back and download the first book in the series<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33876103.Let_s_Be_Just_Friends__Just_Friends___1_" title="Let's Be Just Friends (Just Friends, #1) by Camilla Isley" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1510664476s/33967716.jpg" alt="My Best Friend's Boyfriend (Just Friends, #3) by Camilla Isley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>. I think I'm jumping right into book three because I want to know what will happen with Madison and Haley and the gorgeous Williams brothers...<br><br>I found this book in the friends to lovers lists and since I already liked the author I gave it a try. Seeing the author's review I found out you can get it for free via the author's newsletter signing up here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.camillaisley.com/freebie">http://www.camillaisley.com/freebie</a></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2203689145?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anniek" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anniek" href="/user/show/46780725-anniek">Anniek</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2203689145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1584096638950611918"><br/>Alice has been secretly in love with Jack since the moment she met him. Alice and Jack became best friends and Alice has accepted the fact that this is all she and Jack will ever be. When she and her boyfriend brake up Alice decides that it's time to stop playing around. She makes a move on Jack, but he rejects her and walks away. Alice tries to get back to where they were before, only that isn't as easy as she thought it would be. She doesn't know that her kiss did more to Jack than he's willin</span>
  <span id="freeText1584096638950611918" style="display:none"><br />Alice has been secretly in love with Jack since the moment she met him. Alice and Jack became best friends and Alice has accepted the fact that this is all she and Jack will ever be. When she and her boyfriend brake up Alice decides that it's time to stop playing around. She makes a move on Jack, but he rejects her and walks away. Alice tries to get back to where they were before, only that isn't as easy as she thought it would be. She doesn't know that her kiss did more to Jack than he's willing to admit. Is Jack ready to step out of his comfort zone?<br /><br />Jack has been burned by love in the past and he's determined not to go through anything like that ever again. Jack is not blind and he has always seen how gorgeous Alice is, but he never wanted to take it to the next level before their kiss. At a party Alice meets Jack's team captain and they start dating. Jealousy is eating Jack alive and he can't deny his feelings for Alice any longer. Will he be too late now to do something about what's in his heart?<br /><br />Alice and Jack truly are best friends. They're so comfortable around each other and I liked reading about that. They're standing side by side and are weathering the storms together. It was clear from the start how compatible they'd be as a couple. I love the way Camilla Isley connects the remaining dots of the stories from her first Just Friends book in Friend Zone. I always like to read up on characters that I've previously been introduced to. Camilla Isley never disappoints with her lighthearted romantic novels. She is an experienced and skillful writer and has written another fun and sweet story that I highly recommend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1584096638950611918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1886749098" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1886749098" />
    <a title="Amanda " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5149059-amanda"><img alt="Amanda " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574701938p2/5149059.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1886749098?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda " href="/user/show/5149059-amanda">Amanda </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1886749098&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1886749098" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7428541981355977817">2.5 *Somewhat long review* First, let me say that I got a free pre-order copy of this book by going to Camilla Isley website and entering her newsletter for upcoming books she has coming out. <br/><br/>That being said I did feel this book was a improvement over 'Let's Be Just Friends', which if anyone were to check I gave a negative review for so I wasn't entirely sure that I would like any of the characters in this book. Which was one of many of my pet peeves of that book but before I get into what I did</span>
  <span id="freeText7428541981355977817" style="display:none">2.5 *Somewhat long review* First, let me say that I got a free pre-order copy of this book by going to Camilla Isley website and entering her newsletter for upcoming books she has coming out. <br /><br />That being said I did feel this book was a improvement over 'Let's Be Just Friends', which if anyone were to check I gave a negative review for so I wasn't entirely sure that I would like any of the characters in this book. Which was one of many of my pet peeves of that book but before I get into what I didn't like about this book and why I gave the book the rating I did let me first say what I like about this book. Unlike in 'Let's Be Just Friends' I like the main characters Alice slightly better than Rose and Jack way better than Tyler, the friendship between Alice and Jack was more interesting and you really believe that these two were friends. <br /><br />*SPOILERS AHEAD*<br />The story unfolds when Alice makes a not so good attempt at letting Jack know her real feeling for him by kissing him which understanding he rebuffs, thinking that the only reason she was trying to make a pass at him was do to her a breakup that happened earlier that night. Alice takes his rebuff to mean that he doesn't want a relationship with her when it was really that he didn't want to take advantage of their friendship, she then decides that she's tired of waiting for him to notice her and comes up with a plan to make him jealous. Enter Paul Jack's friend and captain of his basketball team, Alice starts a relationship with Paul and doesn't see her plan to make Jack jealous is working. Her new relationship causes trouble and a rift between the 2 year friendship she has with Jack, I gotta say out of both journeys I prefer Jack's journey of if the feelings he has for Alice is pure friendship or more to Alice 'I'll make Jack jealous by dating his friend' journey. Her friends even tried to warn her that her plan would backfire and it did, Jack was jealous and did try to once to break them up at the start of the relationship but decided that if she really wanted to date Paul that he wouldn't interfere. NEVER date the friend of the person you really want to be with it cause unnecessary drama and makes it seem like you really didn't have deeper feelings for them. <br /><br />Even though I like this book better than the first one, there were still problems I had with this story biggest one is LACK OF COMMUNICATION, Alice spends a great deal of the book dismissing Jack's blatant obvious affects her relationship is having on him and that his feelings for her aren't platonic. Considering how she was once the one who was feeling jealous about the girls Jack would go out with she should have been able to pick up that that's how Jack was reacting to her relationship with Paul. There are other problems but I don't want to give away the entire book let's just say that if something happens before a friendship occurred shouldn't be made into such a big deal once the person finds out. I also wish that none of the characters from the first book made appearance in this book if it weren't for that and the problems I had with the story the rating would be higher.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7428541981355977817" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13688249465060095731">I really enjoyed "Friend Zone" by Camilla Isley. I was given an advance copy to read in exchange for an honest review. The book is the second in a new series based on the premise of best friends falling in love or not in some cases. I've loved everything Camilla has written to date and even though I thought this wasn't her best work - it was still very enjoyable to read. It was well written, I just had a harder time connecting with the characters in this book for some reason. Give it a chance th</span>
  <span id="freeText13688249465060095731" style="display:none">I really enjoyed "Friend Zone" by Camilla Isley. I was given an advance copy to read in exchange for an honest review. The book is the second in a new series based on the premise of best friends falling in love or not in some cases. I've loved everything Camilla has written to date and even though I thought this wasn't her best work - it was still very enjoyable to read. It was well written, I just had a harder time connecting with the characters in this book for some reason. Give it a chance though, it might have been my frame of mind this weekend. Overall, still worth the money.<br />Happy Reading...enjoy!</span>

<div id="review_2432841073" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2432841073" />
    <a title="Kimberly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4855003-kimberly"><img alt="Kimberly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296020986p2/4855003.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2432841073?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kimberly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kimberly" href="/user/show/4855003-kimberly">Kimberly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2432841073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12237715055123748293">I’m happy to say that this installment of the series was leaps and bounds better than the first book. Unlike the last time, this time I really became invested in the characters as the story progressed. The characters had a lot more depth, and the writing flowed much more easily despite a few typos.<br/><br/>This story backtracks a bit from where the last one let off. It follows the story of Alice who is in love with her best friend Jack. Alice, if you’ve read the first book, is Ethan’s ex. The bulk of thi</span>
  <span id="freeText12237715055123748293" style="display:none">I’m happy to say that this installment of the series was leaps and bounds better than the first book. Unlike the last time, this time I really became invested in the characters as the story progressed. The characters had a lot more depth, and the writing flowed much more easily despite a few typos.<br /><br />This story backtracks a bit from where the last one let off. It follows the story of Alice who is in love with her best friend Jack. Alice, if you’ve read the first book, is Ethan’s ex. The bulk of this story takes place soon after Ethan broke up with Alice for Rose, and progresses through to the “wedding from hell.”<br /><br />I really liked how the author weaved a continuation of the first story into this one, giving the reader a small glimpse of what happened with Rose, Ethan, Tyler, and Georgiana. Personally, I still hate Georgiana—while she’s Alice’s friend and “mentor,” she is terrible to her cousin Madison who is Alice’s roommate and friend. The twist at the end was extremely interesting, and I’m curious to see how this will play out in the next book which is about Haley (the other roommate). <br /><br />As for the main characters in this story, I felt they were much more genuine and thought out. The situations were believable and didn’t have me screaming or wanting to strangle the characters. While I would have liked to see more significant interactions between Alice and Jack, it didn’t take anything away from the overall plot that this wasn’t included. I enjoyed watching the different relationship unfold whether it was the friendship between Alice/Madison/Haley or the relationships between Alice/Peter or Alice/Jack. <br /><br />The ending was satisfying enough that I’m curious to read the next installment of this series, particularly since it takes place in the same universe. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12237715055123748293" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1992397107" />
    <a title="Emily" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53413942-emily"><img alt="Emily" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1992397107?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily" href="/user/show/53413942-emily">Emily</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53413942-emily?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1992397107" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13418105780287714877">This book was filled with SO MUCH DRAMA and I was loving it. I really liked the first book in this trilogy 'Let's Just Be Friends' and I was so excited to read more about the characters but this one was more focused on new characters and the characters from book one were only briefly mentioned in the book and came back in the last few chapters. However, I still enjoyed this book!<br/><br/>Likes:<br/>-<b> All The Characters. </b> All the characters had distinct personalities and although they irritated me sometimes wi</span>
  <span id="freeText13418105780287714877" style="display:none">This book was filled with SO MUCH DRAMA and I was loving it. I really liked the first book in this trilogy 'Let's Just Be Friends' and I was so excited to read more about the characters but this one was more focused on new characters and the characters from book one were only briefly mentioned in the book and came back in the last few chapters. However, I still enjoyed this book!<br /><br />Likes:<br />-<b> All The Characters. </b> All the characters had distinct personalities and although they irritated me sometimes with their stupidity, it all ended okay.<br />-<b> Clear Formatting. </b> In the book the chapters alternated the narrator but it was easy to get the hang of it and it was so easy to read. In the beginning I thought it would be difficult to remember who was who, as it seemed that new people were being introduced left right and center. But it was actually really easy and I could draw you a family tree it was so clear.<br />-<b> Writing Style. </b> Camilla Isley has such an easy-going and flowing writing style that just pulls you in and gets you addicted to the story. <br /><br />Dislikes:<br />-<b> Wrong Timing. </b> So many people were in love with each other. The only problem was that they kept missing each other and I was so irritated by it sometimes but I suppose it made the book even better and made me want to keep on reading in hopes people would be together.<br />-<b> Cliches. </b> Some parts I knew what was coming and I felt myself getting bored at some parts. However, there were very few of these moments and I really liked most of it and there were surprises along the way!<br /><br />This book was really light-hearted and I enjoyed it and I need book 3 asap, please and thank you.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DoThmkZwH/k40nXxWszkgNzgb07Vs9WBFgcgofKHdX8L++RV5Zv/0iYJ1X3dRt9sUUP0r210m1PdrTCNhNS/Vg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('a/hMWNkZ6gkR271aKnZK5Cc8oVblmo7vttqqjYPWStRuh0mXevIKIg8AHdat/HEIqp86t11dwD19cLqh9YWA/Q==')})
  }
